Active Mihile's Soul
Master Level 10
Description Summons a spirit that automatically performs an area attack on the enemies you are fighting. Skill level increases by 1 every 15 levels.
Level 1 MP Cost: 11, Damage: 70%, Duration: 110 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.
10 MP Cost: 20, Damage: 160%, Duration: 200 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.

Show/hide all levels
Passive Invincible Belief
Master Level 6
Description Muster your faith in the darkest of times to recover health.
Does not activate in towns or while affected by statuses that prevent HP recovery. Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase buff durations, or modify recovery skill potency.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Warrior job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Automatically activates when your health falls to 15% of your Max HP or below. Restores 20% of Max HP every 1 sec for 3 sec
Cooldown: 410 sec.
6 Automatically activates when your health falls to 15% of your Max HP or below. Restores 35% of Max HP every 1 sec for 3 sec
Cooldown: 210 sec.

Active Leap Attack
Master Level 1
Description Ambush the enemy by rapidly dropping to ground from mid-air.
Can only be used if there's a platform within range below you. Use along with a left or right arrow keys to drop yourself diagonally.
Can also be used by pressing the downward, left, or right arrow keys plus the attack key, instead of manually activating the skill.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5, Damage: 90%, Number of Attacks: 2, Max Enemies Hit: 4

Active Combo Attack
Master Level 1
Description When activated, grants a chance to add each attack to the Combo Orb, up to 5.
Using the skill activates the effect, and using the skill again deactivates it.
Right-click to toggle the Combo Orb Effect on/off
Level 1 When activated, 40% chance of having the attack added to the Combo Count.
Attack Power for each Combo Count: +2, Max Combo Count: 5

Active Spirit Blade
Master Level 20
Description The sword and the spirit are united to improve the Attack Power of party members including yourself for a short time, and reflect a multiple of the damage that you receive.
Level 1 MP Cost: 12, Duration: 86 sec, Attack Power of Party Members Including Yourself: +11
Damage Taken: -11%, Damage Reflection: 120% of damage received.
20 MP Cost: 20, Duration: 200 sec, Attack Power of Party Members Including Yourself: +30
Damage Taken: -30%, Damage Reflection: 500% of damage received.

Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Cooldown: 65 sec

If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.

Active Burning Soul Blade
Master Level 25
Description Conjures a burning soul blade to fight at your side. Unaffected by attack reflection. Use the skill key with the down arrow key to summon it in a fixed state.
With Action Customization enabled, you can immediately summon in a fixed state by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Required Skill: Raging Blow Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 350. Fully charges combo to the max upon casting. Summon Duration: 60 sec. Press the skill key again to have the blade stay put (press it again for it to respawn).
When you use your offensive skill, attacks up to 8 enemies 6 times every 1 sec., with 50% bonus Critical Rate.
Normal - Damage: 332% (While Enraged: 364%)
Stationary - Damage: 301% (While Enraged: 327%)
Cooldown: 120 sec.

Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
